           <h4 class="mh-widget-title">
            <span class="mh-widget-title-inner">
             <a class="mh-widget-title-link" href="https://www.aronline.co.uk/our-cars/">
              Our cars
             </a>
            </span>
           </h4>
           <ul class="mh-custom-posts-widget clearfix">
            <li class="mh-custom-posts-item mh-custom-posts-large clearfix post-164725 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-alexanders-citroen-xm category-our-cars tag-citroen-xm tag-daily-driver tag-featured tag-hydropneumatic">
             <div class="mh-custom-posts-large-inner clearfix">
              <figure class="mh-custom-posts-thumb-xl">
               <a class="mh-thumb-icon mh-thumb-icon-small-mobile" href="https://www.aronline.co.uk/our-cars/alexanders-citroen-xm/our-cars-alexanders-citroen-xm-22000miles-on/" title="Our cars : Alexander’s Citroën XM – 22,000 miles on">
                <img alt="" class="attachment-mh-magazine-medium size-mh-magazine-medium wp-post-image" height="245" sizes="(max-width: 326px) 100vw, 326px" src="https://i2.wp.com/www.aronline.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/xm-featured.jpg?resize=326%2C245&amp;ssl=1" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/www.aronline.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/xm-featured.jpg?resize=678%2C509&amp;ssl=1 678w, https://i2.wp.com/www.aronline.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/xm-featured.jpg?resize=326%2C245&amp;ssl=1 326w, https://i2.wp.com/www.aronline.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/xm-featured.jpg?resize=80%2C60&amp;ssl=1 80w, https://i2.wp.com/www.aronline.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/xm-featured.jpg?zoom=3&amp;resize=326%2C245&amp;ssl=1 978w" width="326"/>
               </a>
              </figure>
              <div class="mh-custom-posts-content">
               <div class="mh-custom-posts-header">
                <h3 class="mh-custom-posts-xl-title">
                 <a href="https://www.aronline.co.uk/our-cars/alexanders-citroen-xm/our-cars-alexanders-citroen-xm-22000miles-on/" title="Our cars : Alexander’s Citroën XM – 22,000 miles on">
                  Our cars : Alexander’s Citroën XM – 22,000 miles on
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="mh-meta entry-meta">
                 <span class="entry-meta-date updated">
                  <i class="fa fa-clock-o">
                  </i>
                  <a href="https://www.aronline.co.uk/2018/04/">
                   10 April 2018
                  </a>
                 </span>
                 <span class="entry-meta-comments">
                  <i class="fa fa-comment-o">
                  </i>
                  <a class="mh-comment-count-link" href="https://www.aronline.co.uk/our-cars/alexanders-citroen-xm/our-cars-alexanders-citroen-xm-22000miles-on/#comments">
                   11
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="mh-excerpt">
                Although the XM is not yet a classic in legal terms, it certainly is rare here in Germany – very
